      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": "from math import radians, cos, sin, asin, sqrt\n\n# Function to calculate distance in KM using Haversine formula\ndef calculate_distance(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2):\n    R = 6371  # Earth radius in km\n    dlat = radians(lat2 - lat1)\n    dlon = radians(lon2 - lon1)\n    a = sin(dlat/2)**2 + cos(radians(lat1)) * cos(radians(lat2)) * sin(dlon/2)**2\n    c = 2 * asin(sqrt(a))\n    return R * c\n\n# Example: pick a launch site (first row of df)\nlaunch_lat = spacex_df.iloc[0]['Lat']\nlaunch_lon = spacex_df.iloc[0]['Long']\n\n# Example: manually add a coastline point (closest coast coordinate, e.g. Miami area)\ncoast_lat, coast_lon = 25.7617, -80.1918\n\n# Calculate distance\ndistance = calculate_distance(launch_lat, launch_lon, coast_lat, coast_lon)\n\n# Add marker for coastline point\ndistance_marker = folium.Marker(\n    [coast_lat, coast_lon],\n    icon=DivIcon(\n        icon_size=(200,36),\n        icon_anchor=(0,0),\n        html=f'<div style=\"font-size:12px; color:#d35400;\"><b>Coastline</b><br>{distance:.2f} KM</div>'\n    )\n)\nsite_map.add_child(distance_marker)\n\n# Draw line between launch site and coastline\ncoordinates = [[launch_lat, launch_lon], [coast_lat, coast_lon]]\nlines = folium.PolyLine(locations=coordinates, weight=2, color='blue')\nsite_map.add_child(lines)\n\n# Show updated map\nsite_map\n",

      "source": "# Example: Launch site coordinates (use first site for demo)\nlaunch_lat = spacex_df.iloc[0]['Lat']\nlaunch_lon = spacex_df.iloc[0]['Long']\n\n# Example: Add closest city, railway, and highway coordinates (you get these from MousePosition plugin)\ncity_lat, city_lon = 28.0836, -80.6081       # Example Melbourne, FL\nrail_lat, rail_lon = 28.5623, -80.5679       # Example railway near Cape Canaveral\nhwy_lat, hwy_lon  = 28.5100, -80.7990        # Example highway near launch site\n\n# 1. Distance calculation\ncity_distance = calculate_distance(launch_lat, launch_lon, city_lat, city_lon)\nrail_distance = calculate_distance(launch_lat, launch_lon, rail_lat, rail_lon)\nhwy_distance  = calculate_distance(launch_lat, launch_lon, hwy_lat, hwy_lon)\n\n# 2. Add Markers\ncity_marker = folium.Marker(\n    [city_lat, city_lon],\n    icon=DivIcon(\n        icon_size=(200,36),\n        icon_anchor=(0,0),\n        html=f'<div style=\"font-size:12px; color:blue;\"><b>City</b><br>{city_distance:.2f} KM</div>'\n    )\n)\n\nrail_marker = folium.Marker(\n    [rail_lat, rail_lon],\n    icon=DivIcon(\n        icon_size=(200,36),\n        icon_anchor=(0,0),\n        html=f'<div style=\"font-size:12px; color:green;\"><b>Railway</b><br>{rail_distance:.2f} KM</div>'\n    )\n)\n\nhwy_marker = folium.Marker(\n    [hwy_lat, hwy_lon],\n    icon=DivIcon(\n        icon_size=(200,36),\n        icon_anchor=(0,0),\n        html=f'<div style=\"font-size:12px; color:red;\"><b>Highway</b><br>{hwy_distance:.2f} KM</div>'\n    )\n)\n\nsite_map.add_child(city_marker)\nsite_map.add_child(rail_marker)\nsite_map.add_child(hwy_marker)\n\n# 3. Draw PolyLines (lines between launch site and each object)\ncity_line = folium.PolyLine([[launch_lat, launch_lon], [city_lat, city_lon]], color=\"blue\", weight=2)\nrail_line = folium.PolyLine([[launch_lat, launch_lon], [rail_lat, rail_lon]], color=\"green\", weight=2)\nhwy_line  = folium.PolyLine([[launch_lat, launch_lon], [hwy_lat, hwy_lon]], color=\"red\", weight=2)\n\nsite_map.add_child(city_line)\nsite_map.add_child(rail_line)\nsite_map.add_child(hwy_line)\n\n# Show updated map\nsite_map\n",
